    );

	 			'http://www.worldcrunch.com/img/worldc-pin.png',

    );

	 		var map_options = {
	 			draggable: false,
	 			zoomControl: false,

	 			zoom: 3,
	 			disableDefaultUI: true,
	 			mapTypeControlOptions: {

	 			}
	 		}
	 		
	 		map = new google.maps.Map(map_canvas, map_options);

	function initialize_fullmapview() {
		
		

		image = new google.maps.MarkerImage(
			'http://www.worldcrunch.com/img/worldc-pin-blue.png',
    new google.maps.Size(30,39),    // size of the image
    new google.maps.Point(0,0), // origin, in this case top-left corner
    new google.maps.Point(9, 25)    // anchor, i.e. the point half-way along the bottom of the image
    );
		imageh = new google.maps.MarkerImage(
			'http://www.worldcrunch.com/img/worldc-pin.png',
    new google.maps.Size(30,39),    // size of the image
    new google.maps.Point(0,0), // origin, in this case top-left corner
    new google.maps.Point(9, 25)    // anchor, i.e. the point half-way along the bottom of the image
    );
		
		
		var styledMap = new google.maps.StyledMapType(styles,{name: 'Styled Map'});
		
		var map_canvas = document.getElementById('map_canvas');
		var map_options = {
			zoomControl: true, 
			disableDoubleClickZoom: true,
			scrollwheel: false, 
			zoom: 3,
			disableDefaultUI: true,
			mapTypeControlOptions: {
				mapTypeIds: [google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP, 'map_style']
			}
		}
		
		map = new google.maps.Map(map_canvas, map_options);
		map.mapTypes.set('map_style', styledMap);
		map.setMapTypeId('map_style');
		google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'click', function(event) {
			$('#fullmap_art').fadeOut('slow');
			for (var i=0; i&lt;arrayOfMarkers.length;i++) {
				arrayOfMarkers[i].setIcon(image);
			}
			
			map.setZoom(3);
		});
			 //Polyline();
		//map.panBy(0,-172);
		map.setCenter(new google.maps.LatLng(0,0));

		newmarkercontentSM(male[0][2]);
		$('#fullmap_art').fadeIn('slow');
		$('#fullmap_art').css('z-index','10000');
		$('#fullmap_art').css('position','relative');

		
	}
	
			function initialize_mondo(first_time) {
			
			var ft = true;
			if(first_time!=null || first_time!= ""){
				ft = first_time;
			}

			image = new google.maps.MarkerImage(
				'http://www.worldcrunch.com/img/worldc-pin-blue.png',
    new google.maps.Size(30,39),    // size of the image
    new google.maps.Point(0,0), // origin, in this case top-left corner
    new google.maps.Point(9, 25)    // anchor, i.e. the point half-way along the bottom of the image
    );
			
			imageh = new google.maps.MarkerImage(
				'http://www.worldcrunch.com/img/worldc-pin.png',
    new google.maps.Size(30,39),    // size of the image
    new google.maps.Point(0,0), // origin, in this case top-left corner
    new google.maps.Point(9, 25)    // anchor, i.e. the point half-way along the bottom of the image
    );
			
			var styledMap = new google.maps.StyledMapType(styles,{name: 'Styled Map'});
			
			var map_canvas = document.getElementById('map_canvas');
			var map_options = {
				scrollwheel: false, 
				center: new google.maps.LatLng(0, 0),
				disableDoubleClickZoom: false,
				zoom: 3,
				zoomControl: true,
				zoomControlOptions: {
					style: google.maps.ZoomControlStyle.SMALL,
					position: google.maps.ControlPosition.LEFT_CENTER
				},
				disableDefaultUI: true,
				mapTypeControlOptions: {
					mapTypeIds: [google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP, 'map_style']
				}
			}
			
			map = new google.maps.Map(map_canvas, map_options);
			map.mapTypes.set('map_style', styledMap);
			map.setMapTypeId('map_style');
			
			 //Polyline();
		//map.panBy(0,-130);
		
		map.setCenter(new google.maps.LatLng(100,0));
		google.maps.event.addListenerOnce(map, 'tilesloaded', function(){
    //this part runs when the mapobject is created and rendered
    var scrollTop = parseInt($('html').css('top'));
    $('html').removeClass('noscroll');
    $('html,body').scrollTop(-scrollTop);
    
        	
    });
	}

			function initialize_mondo1() {

				var mm = com.modestmaps;
				var dmap = document.getElementById('map_canvas');
				wax.tilejson('http://a.tiles.mapbox.com/v3/examples.map-vyofok3q.jsonp',
					function(tj) {
						map = new com.modestmaps.Map(dmap,
							new wax.mm.connector(tj), null, [
							easey_handlers.DragHandler(),
							easey_handlers.TouchHandler(),
							easey_handlers.DoubleClickHandler()
							]);
						
						map.setCenterZoom(new com.modestmaps.Location(0, 0), 3);

						map.addCallback('zoomed', function() {
            // console.log(map.getZoom());
        });


					});
				
			}
						
			function smoothZoom (map, max, cnt) {
				if (cnt &gt;= max) {
					return;
				}
				else {
					z = google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'zoom_changed', function(event){
						google.maps.event.removeListener(z);
						self.smoothZoom(map, max, cnt + 1);
					});
        setTimeout(function(){map.setZoom(cnt)}, 80); // 80ms is what I found to work well on my system -- it might not work well on all systems
    }
}

		}

                    //map.addOverlay(marker); zamena ...
                    
                    marker.setMap(map);
					//arrayOfMarkers[i] = marker;

				}
				
				function addMarker_mondo(){ 
					
					for (i=0;i&lt;male.length;i++){

                    //map.addOverlay(marker); zamena ...
                    

                    marker.setMap(map);
                    
                    arrayOfMarkers[i] = marker;

				}
				
				
			}
			
			function addMarker_carousel(){ 
				
				for (i=0;i&lt;male.length;i++){
					var markerPoint = new google.maps.LatLng(male[i][0], male[i][1]);
					var windowInfo= male[i][2];
					var marker = new createMarker_carousel(markerPoint,windowInfo,male[i][3],male[i][4]);
                    //map.addOverlay(marker); zamena ...
                    
                    marker.setMap(map);
                    
                    arrayOfMarkers[i] = marker;
					// ...
				}
				
				
			}
			
			
			function addMarker_fullmap(male){ 
               //alert(male.length)

               for (i=0;i&lt;male.length;i++){
               	
               	if(male[i][0] == "" &amp;&amp; male[i][1] == ""){
               		male[i][0]  = 0;
               		male[i][1] = 0;}
               		
               		var markerPoint = new google.maps.LatLng(male[i][0], male[i][1]);
               		var windowInfo= male[i][2];
               		var marker = new createMarker_fullmap(markerPoint,windowInfo,male[i][3],male[i][4],windowInfo);
                    //map.addOverlay(marker); zamena ...
                    
                    marker.setMap(map);
                    
                    arrayOfMarkers[i] = marker;
                }
					// ...
					
					
					
				}
				
				function createMarker_carousel(male, overlayText,zoom,pos,id) {
		// zamena .... GMarker i promena vo atributite
		var marker = new google.maps.Marker({
			position: male,
			icon: image
		});
		   // zamena .... GEvent
           //google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', function() { map_popup(overlayText,male,zoom,pos);  changepin_img(marker);});
           
           
           
           
           return marker;
       }

       function createMarker(male, overlayText,zoom,pos,id) {
		// zamena .... GMarker i promena vo atributite
		var marker = new google.maps.Marker({
			position: male,
			icon: image
		});
		   // zamena .... GEvent
           //google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', function() { map_popup(overlayText,male,zoom,pos);  changepin_img(marker);});
           google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', function() {
           	
           	for (var i=0; i&lt;arrayOfMarkers.length;i++) {
           		arrayOfMarkers[i].setIcon(image);
           	}
           	
           	var divpos = pos - 1; 
           	marker.setIcon(imageh);
           	console.log("log div position "+divpos);
					//$.scrollTo($('#art'+divpos), 500, {offsetTop: '-250px'});
					
					$art = $('.artclass').first();
					$('html,body').animate({
						scrollTop: $art.offset().top - 700 }, 200);
					$('html,body').animate({
						scrollTop: $('#art'+divpos).offset().top}, 1000);
					
					
					newmarkercontent(male,id);
					
				});
           
           
           
           return marker;
       }

       function createMarker_fullmap(male, overlayText,zoom,pos,id) {
		// zamena .... GMarker i promena vo atributite
		var marker = new google.maps.Marker({
			position: male,
			icon: image
		});
		   // zamena .... GEvent
           //google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', function() { map_popup(overlayText,male,zoom,pos);  changepin_img(marker);});
           google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', function() {
           	
           	for (var i=0; i&lt;arrayOfMarkers.length;i++) {
           		arrayOfMarkers[i].setIcon(image);
           	}
           	
           	var divpos = pos - 1; 
           	marker.setIcon(imageh);
					//$.scrollTo($('#art'+divpos), 500, {offsetTop: '-250px'});
					
					
					newmarkercontent(male,id);
					
				});
           
           
           
           return marker;
       }

       function reload_map(x1,y1){

          map.panTo(new google.maps.LatLng(x1,y1)); 
          map.panBy(410,85);

		//map.panBy(350,10);
		
	}

	function lockscroll(){
		
		if ($(document).height() &gt; $(window).height()) {
     var scrollTop = ($('html').scrollTop()) ? $('html').scrollTop() : $('body').scrollTop(); // Works for Chrome, Firefox, IE...
     $('html').addClass('noscroll').css('top',-scrollTop);         
 }

}

function newmarkercontent(male,id){



   map.panTo(male);
   map.setZoom(4);



   var result = (90 / 100) * screen.width;
			//alert("div "+result+"="+ div.offsetWidth);
			//alert($(window).width());

			if ($(window).width() &lt;= 1100  ){	
				//alert($(window).width());
				map.panBy(460,215);
			}

			if ($(window).width() &gt;= 1100  &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &lt;= 1200  ){	
				//alert($(window).width());
				map.panBy(520,215);
			}	
			else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1200 &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &lt;= 1300 ){	
				//alert($(window).width());
				map.panBy(580,215);
			}
			else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1300 &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &lt;= 1400 ){	
				//alert($(window).width());
				map.panBy(640,215);
			}
			else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1400 &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &lt;= 1500 ){	
				//alert($(window).width());
				map.panBy(650,215);
			}

			else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1500 &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &lt;= 1600 ){	
				//alert($(window).width());
				map.panBy(710,215);
			}
			else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1600 &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &lt;= 1750 ){	
				//alert($(window).width());
				map.panBy(790,215);
			}

			else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1750 &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &lt;= 1950 ){	
				//alert($(window).width());
				map.panBy(890,215);
			}

			else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1750){	
				//alert($(window).width());
				map.panBy(1300,215);
			}
			
			$('#fullmap_art').fadeIn('slow');
			$('#fullmap_art').css('z-index','10000');
			$('#fullmap_art').css('position','relative');
			
			//alert(id);
			 $.get('http://www.worldcrunch.com/ajax/hp_subcontent.php?id='+id, function(data){ 
			 	
			 	obj = jQuery.parseJSON(data);
			 	
			// alert(obj.title);
			if(obj.ribbon != ""){
				$('.caption').html(obj.ribbon+'&lt;img src="http://www.worldcrunch.com/img/bg-fold.png" width="11" height="37" alt="background"&gt;');
			}
			$('#fullmap_art_title').html(obj.title);
			$('#fullmap_art_img').attr('src',obj.img); 
			$('.location').html(obj.state);
			$('#sharepopup-00').html('&lt;div class="addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style addthis_32x32_style " addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_preferred_1" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_preferred_2" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_preferred_3" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_preferred_4" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_compact" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
			$('#readmore-fullmapart').attr('href',obj.url);
			$('#url-tile').attr('href',obj.url);
			addthis.toolbox("#sharepopup-00");
			
		});

}

function Click(id){
	
	gift_val = $( "#gift" ).val();
	vaucher_val = $( "#vaucher" ).val();
	if(id==1){ window.location = "http://www.worldcrunch.com/subscribe.php?pr-subscription-length=monthly&amp;gift="+gift_val+"&amp;vaucher="+vaucher_val;}
	if(id==2){ window.location ="http://www.worldcrunch.com/subscribe.php?pr-subscription-length=sixmonths&amp;gift="+gift_val+"&amp;vaucher="+vaucher_val;}
	if(id==3){ window.location ="http://www.worldcrunch.com/subscribe.php?pr-subscription-length=twelvemonths&amp;gift="+gift_val+"&amp;vaucher="+vaucher_val;} 

}

function nextPoint(i) {

  $("#fullmap_art").fadeOut();
  $("#fullmap_art").fadeIn(); 
  map.panTo(new google.maps.LatLng(male[i][0], male[i][1]));
		//setTimeout(function() { $("#fullmap_art").fadeIn("slow"); map.panTo(new google.maps.LatLng(male[i][0], male[i][1]));map.panBy(458,110); }, 500); 
		//Smoothpan(lastloc,newloc);
	//	map.panBy(458,110);
	



	if(!trigger){

		map.setZoom(4);

		if ( $(window).width() &lt;= 1200){	
					//alert($(window).width());
					map.panBy(460,110);
				}	
				else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1200 &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &lt;= 1400 ){	
					//alert($(window).width());
					map.panBy(460,110);
				}
				else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1400 &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &lt;= 1600 ){	
					//alert($(window).width());
					map.panBy(630,110);
				}
				else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1600){	
					//alert($(window).width());
					map.panBy(790,110);
				}
			}else{
				if ( $(window).width() &lt;= 1200){	
					//alert($(window).width());
					map.panBy(460,215);
				}	
				else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1200 &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &lt;= 1400 ){	
					//alert($(window).width());
					map.panBy(460,215);
				}
				else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1400 &amp;&amp; $(window).width() &lt;= 1600 ){	
					//alert($(window).width());
					map.panBy(630,215);
				}
				else if ( $(window).width() &gt;= 1600){	
					//alert($(window).width());
					map.panBy(790,215);
				}
			}

		//map.setZoom(3);
		newmarkercontentSM(male[i][2]);
		$(".newsmap-page").removeClass("page-active");
		$("#cont"+i).addClass("page-active");
	}

		function newmarkercontentSM(id){
			

			
			 $.get('http://www.worldcrunch.com/ajax/hp_subcontent.php?id='+id, function(data){ 
			 	
			 	obj = jQuery.parseJSON(data);
			 	
			// alert(obj.title);
			if(obj.ribbon != ""){
				$('.caption').html(obj.ribbon+'&lt;img src="http://www.worldcrunch.com/img/bg-fold.png" width="11" height="37" alt="background"&gt;');
			}
			$('#fullmap_art_title').html(obj.title);
			$('#fullmap_art_img').attr('src',obj.img); 
			$('.location').html(obj.state);
			$('#sharepopup-00').html('&lt;div class="addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style addthis_32x32_style " addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;div class="share-social"&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_facebook" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_twitter" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_linkedin" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_google_plusone_share" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_reddit" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_email" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="read-later"&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_kindleit" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_pocket" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a class="addthis_button_email" addthis:url="'+obj.url+'" addthis:title="'+obj.title+'"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
			$('#readmore-fullmapart').attr('href',obj.url);
			$('#url-tile').attr('href',obj.url);
			addthis.toolbox("#sharepopup-00");
			

		});

}

var q = 0;

var shown = 1;

function calltimer(shown){
	  timer = setTimeout(function() {   //calls click event after a certain time
	  	
	  	
	  	if(shown &gt;= male.length){
	  		
	  		shown = 0;
	  	}
			//alert(shown);
			if(onmouseover == true){
				
				clearTimeout(timer);
				
			}
			else{
				console.log(shown);
				console.log(timer);
				nextPoint(shown);
				shown++;
				calltimer(shown);
			//alert(shown);
		}
		
		if(onmouseover == false){
			//setTimeout(timer);
			
		}
		
		
		
	}, 7000);
	}
	
	function stopartanimation(){
		
		onmouseover = true;
		timer = "";
		clearTimeout(timer);
		
	}
	
	function startartanimation(){
		
		onmouseover = false;
		timer = "";
			//shown = 0;
			calltimer(shown);
			
		}

$(function(){$('.newsmap-page2').click(function() {
	
	if(ok == true){
		//$('#title').hide();
		ok=false;
		//$('#title').toggle( "slide",{direction: 'left'}, 1000*2);
		story = story + 1;
		
		if(story &gt;= male.length-1){
			story = 0;
		}
		
		
		$.ajax({
			url: "http://www.worldcrunch.com/subcontentajax.php?id="+male[story][2],
			type: "get",
			success: function(data){	
				
				
				
				obj = jQuery.parseJSON(data);
				map.panTo(new google.maps.LatLng(male[story][0],male[story][1])); 
				map.panBy(410,85);
				$('#title').toggle( "slide",{direction: 'right'}, 1000,function() {
					$('#title').toggle( "slide",{direction: 'left'}, 1000,function() {ok=true});
					$('#title').html(obj.title);
					
				});
				
				
				
				
				
				
			},
			error:function(){
				alert("failure");

          }   

      });
	}
	
	
	
});

});




var i = 0;
var carosel;
var trigger = false;

function setCookie(c_name,value,exdays)
{

	document.cookie = c_name + '=;expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT;';
	var exdate=new Date();
	exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);

	var c_value=escape(value) + ((exdays==null) ? "" : "; expires="+exdate.toUTCString()+";path=/;Domain=.worldcrunch.com; HttpOnly");
	document.cookie=c_name + "=" + c_value;
}



function getCookie(c_name)
{
	var c_value = document.cookie;
	var c_start = c_value.indexOf(" " + c_name + "=");
	if (c_start == -1)
	{
		c_start = c_value.indexOf(c_name + "=");
	}
	if (c_start == -1)
	{
		c_value = null;
	}
	else
	{
		c_start = c_value.indexOf("=", c_start) + 1;
		var c_end = c_value.indexOf(";", c_start);
		if (c_end == -1)
		{
			c_end = c_value.length;
		}
		c_value = unescape(c_value.substring(c_start,c_end));
	}
	return c_value;
}

function checkCookie()
{
	var mt=getCookie("maptriger");
	if (mt!=null &amp;&amp; mt!="")
	{
 // alert("Welcome again " + username);
}
else 
{
	mt="false";
	if (mt!=null &amp;&amp; mt!="")
	{
		setCookie("maptriger",mt,365);
	}
}
}

// login validation of registration
$("#userlogin").submit(function(event) {


    var thedata = $('#userlogin').serialize();

    event.preventDefault();

    var reqerror = 0;
    var req_error_text = "";
    $.ajaxSetup({
        error: function(jqXHR, exception) {
            if (jqXHR.status === 0) {
                reqerror++;
                req_error_text = "Not connect.\n Verify Network.";
                        // alert('Not connect.\n Verify Network.');
                    } else if (jqXHR.status == 404) {
                        reqerror++;
                        req_error_text = "Requested page not found. [404]";
                        // alert('Requested page not found. [404]');
                    } else if (jqXHR.status == 500) {
                        reqerror++;
                        req_error_text = "Internal Server Error [500].";
                        // alert('Internal Server Error [500].');
                    } else if (exception === 'parsererror') {
                        reqerror++;
                        req_error_text = "Requested JSON parse failed.";
                        // alert('Requested JSON parse failed.');
                    } else if (exception === 'timeout') {
                        reqerror++;
                        req_error_text = "Time out error.";
                        //alert('Time out error.');
                    } else if (exception === 'abort') {
                        reqerror++;
                        req_error_text = "Ajax request aborted.";
                        // alert('Ajax request aborted.');
                    } else {
                        reqerror++;
                        req_error_text = 'Uncaught Error.\n' + jqXHR.responseText;
                        // alert('Uncaught Error.\n' + jqXHR.responseText);
                    }
                }
            });

 $.ajax({
    url: "http://www.worldcrunch.com/flogincheck1.php",
    type: "POST",
    data: thedata,
    success: function(data) {
        if (reqerror &gt; 0) {
            $('#errormsgcomp').html(req_error_text + " Please try again");
        } else {


            $('#errormsglogin').html(data);
            $('#errormsglogin').fadeIn("slow");
            $('#errormsglogin').delay(4000).fadeOut("slow");
            if (data == "Login successful!") {
                $('#errormsglogin').css("background", "-webkit-linear-gradient(top,#1CDF1C,#74D51B)");

                setTimeout(function() {

                    var proverka = $("#head_loc").val();
                    window.location = "http://www.worldcrunch.com/" + $("#head_loc").val();
                    console.log('Ova e proverka: ' + proverka);
                }, 6000);
            }
        }

    },
    error: function() {

                    //$('#infosucess').html('    !');
                    //$('#infosucess').show("slow");
                }
            });
});

// first validation of registration

$(document).ready(function() {


    $("#register").submit(function(event) {


        var thedata = $('#register').serialize();

        event.preventDefault();

        $.ajax({
            url: "http://www.worldcrunch.com/ajax/validatereg.php",
            type: "POST",
            data: thedata,
            success: function(data) {

                if (data == "True") {

                    var page1 = $('.back');
                    var page2 = $('.complete');
                    var toHide = page1.is(':visible') ? page1 : page2;
                    var toShow = page2.is(':visible') ? page1 : page2;

                    toHide.removeClass('flip in').addClass('flip out').hide();
                    toShow.removeClass('flip out').addClass('flip in').show();

                    var popMargTop = ($(loginBox).height() + 24) / 2;
                    var popMargLeft = ($(loginBox).width() + 24) / 2;

                    $(loginBox).css({
                        'margin-top': -popMargTop,
                        'margin-left': -popMargLeft
                    });


                }
                else {
                    $('#errormsgreg').html(data);
                    $('#errormsgreg').fadeIn("slow");
                    $('#errormsgreg').delay(4000).fadeOut("slow");
                }

                    // $('#infosucess').fadeIn(1000);
                    // $('#infosucess').fadeOut(1000*3);
                },
                error: function() {

                    //$('#infosucess').html('    !');
                    //$('#infosucess').show("slow");
                }
            });
});

    // login popup window opening

    $(document).ready(function() {
        $('#login1').click(function() {

            //Getting the variable's value from a link 
            loginBox = $(this).attr('href');

            //Fade in the Popup
            $(loginBox).fadeIn(500);

            //Set the center alignment padding + border see css style
            var popMargTop = ($(loginBox).height() + 24) / 2;
            if ($(loginBox).height() &gt; 1000) {
                var popMargLeft = 500;
            }
            else {
                var popMargLeft = ($(loginBox).width() + 24) / 2;
            }

            $(loginBox).css({
                'margin-top': -popMargTop,
                'margin-left': -popMargLeft
            });

            // Add the mask to body
            $('body').append('&lt;div id="mask"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
            $('#mask').fadeIn(500);

            $(".back").css("display", "none");
            $(".complete").css("display", "none");
            $(".fb-login").html('&lt;a href="https://www.facebook.com/dialog/oauth?client_id=192284580905748&amp;redirect_uri=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.worldcrunch.com%2Fcheck.php%3Fid%3Dfb%26head_loc%3D%2Flogin&amp;state=382becd017acd633cb2be74c52fe4737&amp;scope=email%2C+user_birthday%2C+user_location%2C+user_hometown"&gt;&lt;img src="img/button-connect-fb.png" alt="Connect to your Facebook Account"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;b&gt;Or&lt;/b&gt;');
            //$(".front").css("display","block");

            var page1 = $('.front');
            var toShow = page1;
            toShow.removeClass('flip out').addClass('flip in').show();

            return false;


        });

// When clicking on the button close or the mask layer the popup closed
$('a.close, #mask').click(function() {
    $('#mask , .login-popup').fadeOut(300, function() {
        $('#mask').remove();
    });
    return false;
});

// sliding to sign up in popup

$('.signupbutton').click(function() {
    var page1 = $('.front');
    var page2 = $('.back');
    var toHide = page1.is(':visible') ? page1 : page2;
    var toShow = page2.is(':visible') ? page1 : page2;

    toHide.removeClass('flip in').addClass('flip out').hide();
    toShow.removeClass('flip out').addClass('flip in').show();

    var popMargTop = ($(loginBox).height() + 24) / 2;
    var popMargLeft = ($(loginBox).width() + 24) / 2;

    $(loginBox).css({
        'margin-top': -popMargTop,
        'margin-left': -popMargLeft
    });

});

// sliding back to signin in popup
$('.link-help').click(function() {
    var page1 = $('.front');
    var page2 = $('.back');
    var toHide = page1.is(':visible') ? page1 : page2;
    var toShow = page2.is(':visible') ? page1 : page2;

    toHide.removeClass('flip in').addClass('flip out').hide();
    toShow.removeClass('flip out').addClass('flip in').show();
});


$("#forgotpass").click(function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    $("#userlogin").css("display", "none");
    $("#userForgot").css("display", "block");
    $("#forgotpass").css("display", "none");

});


});
    </script>

 $("#reg_btn_ensta").click(function(event) {
    event.preventDefault();


    $.get("http://www.worldcrunch.com/check.php", $("#ensta_login").serialize())
    .done(function(data) {
        console.log("Data Loaded: " + data);

        var str = data;
        var res = str.split(";");
        if (res[0] == "ok") {
            if (res[1] == "new") {
                $(function() {

                    _gaq.push(['_trackPageview']);
                    _gaq.push(['_trackEvent',
                        'New Registration', // category of activity
                        'ensta-web', // Action
                        ]);

                });
                setTimeout(function() {
                    location.href = res[2];
                }, 1000);
            } else {
                setTimeout(function() {
                    location.href = res[2];
                }, 1000);
            }
            // 
        } else {
            $("#ensta_error").show();
        }

    });
});


});
      </script>

     <header>
      <h1>
       Shanghai's Tale Of Three Towers
      </h1>
      <h2>
       <i>
        In the early 1990s, planners in Shanghai envisioned a trio of mammoth skyscrapers that would symbolize the Chinese citys rebirth. Nearly 20 years later, two of those towers are built. The third is 109 stories to go. Our writer strolls through this 21st century megapolis.
       </i>
      </h2>
      <div class="sharepopup" id="sharepopup-">
       <!-- AddThis Button BEGIN -->
       <div addthis:title="Shanghai's Tale Of Three Towers" addthis:url="http://www.worldcrunch.com/business-finance/shanghai-s-tale-of-three-towers/c2s4452/" class="addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style addthis_32x32_style ">

       <span class="name">
        Frdric Thrin (2012-01-11)
       </span>

      <div class="image-wrapper">
       <img alt="Article illustrative image" class="article-img" height="100%" src="http://static1.worldcrunch.com/images/story/shanghai.JPG" width="100%"/>
       <a href="http://www.worldcrunch.com/source-partner/le-temps-17.html">
        <img alt="Partner logo" class="article-partner" src="http://www.worldcrunch.com/images/partners-bubbles/letemps.png"/>
       </a>
       <span class="caption">
        View from the Shanghai World Financial Center (tyler_haglund)
       </span>

     <div class="artbody">
      <p>
       <strong>
        SHANGHAI
       </strong>
        Shanghai  Tower will eventually be a sight to behold. But right now its nothing more than an ugly concrete cube  15 floors worth, surrounded by steel girders. Hundreds of workers mill about the construction site, which is tucked in amid freeways. Passersby  women clad in pretty ensembles and elegantly dressed businessmen  dont even glance at the imposing sight. Residents of Chinas economic capital are used to seeing buildings crop up like mushrooms in a rainy autumn forest.
      </p>
      <p>
       And yet this skyscraper marks the apotheosis of a daring project launched by Chinese authorities nearly two decades ago. It was 1993 when plans were unveiled to build three giant towers that would symbolize past, present and future. The first of the three behemoths was christened Jim Mao Tower, the second the Shanghai World Financial Center, and the third Shanghai Tower. All three were to be built on a piece of land that otherwise was home to run-down buildings and rice fields.
      </p>
      <p>
       In the early 1990s, Pudong, as this particular area is called, didnt look very promising. While neighborhoods on the other side of the Huangpu River were developing quickly, this space interested no one. Central authorities decided to transform the zone into nothing less than a gigantic business quarter that could vie with Hong Kong or Singapore. And as is often the case in China, there was no pussy-footing around when authorities decided to move ahead with the project.
      </p>
      <p>
       To attract promoters, the city financed construction of a 486-meter (1,535.5-foot) TV tower. The Oriental Pearl Tower resembles a giant display building comprised of three spheres of differing sizes linked by thick tubes of roughly-finished concrete. At night, it becomes a piece of illuminatedkitsch like the boats plying the river  in strident colors: candy pink, neon green, electric blue. Charming? The Chinese seem to like it. Every year, the tower  a symbol of Shanghais renewal  is visited by 3 million people.
      </p>
      <p>
       <strong>
        A skyscraping triumvirate
       </strong>
      </p>
      <p>
       But the tower was just a first step. Hoping to impress lovers of beautiful architecture  which the Oriental Pearl Tower is not  the City of Shanghai decided to call on the best architectural firms to build the first of the three skyscrapers that would incarnate the rebirth of a great city. The result, Jim Mao Tower, is a genuine success. Designed according to the principles of Feng Shui, the 88-story tower (8 = prosperity) was the highest building in China when it was inaugurated in 1998.
      </p>
      <p>
       Ten years later, the Shanghai World Financial  Tower  at 492 meters (1,614 feet)  robbed it of that honor. Nicknamed the bottle opener because of its shape, the billion-dollar tower was originally supposed to feature a round aperture at the summit. But Shanghai residents felt that the design was too reminiscent of the Japanese flag, so the (Japanese) construction company in charge of the project had to change the design.
      </p>
      <p>
       After 9/11, engineers also had to tweak the concept to accommodate empty floors on seven levels where people could gather in the event of fire or other catastrophe. On the 90
       <sup>
        th
       </sup>
       floor, at an extra cost of $200 million, two huge counterweights weighing 150 tons each were installed so that the tower wouldnt move too much during stormy weather.
      </p>
      <p>
       Shanghai Tower will be even more technological. Designed by the American firm Gensler, its concept comprises nine central tubular structures posed one on top of the other, enveloped by a spiral glass casing that is supposed to act like a thermos, preserving the evening cool during the summer months and afternoon warmth during the winter. Huge green spaces, a rainwater recovery system and wind turbines on the roof should mean considerable energy savings for the 632-meter (2,073-foot), 124-story building. An ecological future even in China.
      </p>
      <p>
       <strong>
        Slowing sinking in
       </strong>
      </p>
      <p>
       Shanghais high rise building boom has also had some misses. Another tower, Tomorrow Square in the Puxi district, is indescribably ugly. In some cases, the developments have also been preceded by wide scale demolition  colonial neighborhoods have been razed to make room for unattractive apartment buildings and freeways.
      </p>
      <p>
       In the heart of the city, nine lanes crisscross each other around a central pillar representing nine dragons. And the citys rapid expansion shows no signs of slowing down. There are 12,000 buildings in Shanghai  two new ones are inaugurated every single day, says Tan Ronghua, a local guide.
      </p>
      <p>
       The first bridge crossing the river to Pudong was inaugurated in 1994. Today, there are six bridges and 27 tunnels. But you need that because 20% of the citys 18.5 million inhabitants now live here and they need to be able to get around, he adds.
      </p>
      <p>
       This construction fever also harbors dangers. Built in a water-gorged seismic zone, the city is sinking at the rate of one centimeter per year. In his book
       <em>
        Empire of the Sun,
       </em>
       James Graham Ballard evoked the decadence of Shanghai in the 1930s, a city described as living only in an intense present with no thought of tomorrow.Along the banks of the Huangpu, thats probably about the only thing that hasnt changed in the last eight decades.
      </p>
      <p>
       Read
       <a href="http://www.letemps.ch">
        more
       </a>
       from Le Temps in French
      </p>
      <p>
       Photo -
       <a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/haglundt/5089831900/sizes/l/in/photostream/">
        tyler_haglund
       </a>
      </p>
     </div>

     </div>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(function(){

        $( "#show_newsletter" ).click(function() {
          $( "#subscribe_newsletter" ).slideToggle();
        });

        $( "#postnewsletter" ).submit(function( event ) {
 
          // Stop form from submitting normally
          event.preventDefault();
 
          
          url =  "/ajax/newsletter.php" ;
 
  // Send the data using post
        var posting = $.post( url, $( "#postnewsletter" ).serialize() );
 
      // Put the results in a div
        posting.done(function( data ) {
            $("#newsletter_rez").html(data);
            $("#newsletter_rez").slideToggle();
            setTimeout(function() { $("#newsletter_rez").slideToggle(); }, 20000);
          });
        });

      });

    		2                    // Sets the scope to session-level.  Optional parameter.
    		]);
_gaq.push(['_trackEvent',
	'Shopping', // category of activity
	'hitpaywall', // Action
	]);
  </script>
